Autumn Cocoon Cocoonage Too High: All Industries Dare Not Buy, Especially Zhejiang Road Is Inferior: Request Change of Standards 106

After the National Economic Commission stipulated the standard price of autumn cocoons, the silk control agencies of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces followed the order. Silk manufacturers requested a change, but were not accepted. After the cocoon firms opened the weighing scale, they did not dare to buy in large quantities due to the excessive cocoonage. The details are recorded as follows:

Request for Change: Cocoon Price Is Not Accurate

The Silk Improvement Committee of the National Economic Commission stipulated the cocoon price standard for autumn cocoons in Jiangsu and Zhejiang. According to the New York and Yokohama futures converted into national currency, the average price of silk was set at 670 yuan per dan, and cocoonage work was set at 80 yuan per dan, and cocoon purchasing and drying expenses were 26 yuan. Drying loss was 290 catties, and the cocoon price was calculated according to the size of the cocoonage. For example, if the cocoonage is 460 catties, then each city dan of fresh cocoons is 29 yuan. If the cocoonage is 500 catties, then each city dan of fresh cocoons is 26 yuan. The silk manufacturers in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, in view of the current export price of Chinese silk being 600 yuan and the domestic sales being 620 yuan, which is 60 to 70 yuan different from the 670 yuan set by the Economic Commission, requested a change in history, but were rejected.

Poor Autumn Cocoon Harvest: Reduced Collection Amount

After the autumn cocoons in Jiangsu and Zhejiang were put on the market, all silk factories and surplus cocoon merchants approved and registered by the silk control agencies of the two provinces borrowed from banks and money shops to issue purchases. Autumn cocoons in Zhejiang, Hai Ning, Shuang Lin, Tongxiang, Jiaxing, and other places have had poor harvests due to withered mulberry leaves and weather conditions, and the cocoons are of poor quality. Its cocoonage is more than 900 catties. If purchased according to the standard cocoon price, it will inevitably be costly, so each cocoon firm does not dare to buy in large quantities. At the same time, some silk manufacturers would rather use up the cocoon purchasing expenses than open the scale to buy.

Hydrographic Survey Bureau: Sounding the Yangtze River North Mouth: Counting Two Departments, Hydrographic and Coastal: Drawing Accurate Nautical Charts 107

In view of the fact that the sea surface from the mouth of the Yangtze River to Haizhou is full of shoals and hidden reefs, the Hydrographic Survey Bureau, in order to facilitate the navigation industry, carried out sounding this year. The sounding project is divided into two parts: hydrographic and coastal. Most of the coastline survey has been completed, and the hydrographic sounding will begin soon. However, because the coastline is hundreds of miles long and sparsely populated, the work is very inconvenient. The bureau plans to complete all the work within next year, and will soon send a survey ship to carry out the initial sounding. After the initial sounding is completed, it will be re-measured, and then a hydrographic blueprint will be drawn up based on the sounding results for reference by the navigation industry. The section of the waterway has no accurate nautical chart, so the navigation industry regards it as a daunting task, which greatly affects the development of all industries along the coast.

Qiu Longnu's Disappearance Is Bizarre: One Accuses of Abducting Her Sister, One Accuses of Hiding His Wife 108

Qiu Mingzhu from Xinghua used to live in the countryside, cultivating the fields. Qiu has a younger sister named Longnu, who is 21 years old this year. In the past, she was betrothed to a local man named Wei through a matchmaker. Unexpectedly, Longnu suddenly disappeared, and it has been six years since then, with no trace after searching everywhere. Because the Wei family is urging her to marry, Qiu led his younger brother Minghua to Shanghai, renting a residence at No. 52 Xiangcun Lane, Qu Zhenren Road, Nanshi (pulling a cart in the city during the day to make a living, but still paying attention to finding his sister in his spare time. For several months, there has been no news. Until the evening of the day before yesterday, Chen Guangfa (29 years old) from Yancheng came to Qiu's house to visit. Qiu, who was not acquainted with him, became suspicious. When Qiu extended an invitation to talk with each other, he learned that Chen Guangfa had married Longnu, and Chen was also looking for his suddenly disappeared wife for many days, but there was no trace. He then learned that Longnu had two brothers pulling carts in Shanghai and came to inquire about the whereabouts of his runaway wife. Qiu said that his sister had disappeared in the village six years ago, and he had sent out scouts everywhere, but there was no clue. Now, a brother-in-law suddenly came here, and the situation was even more suspicious. After negotiating with him, Chen also suspected that his wife was hidden by Qiu, and the two sides had a big conflict. After persuasion, they avoided the dispute. Unexpectedly, on the evening of the day before yesterday, Chen suddenly reported to the local police, who took Qiu Mingzhu and his sister Longnu, as well as the related Wang A'er, Chen Xu's, Xu Desheng, Wen Daoming, and other men and women, six people in total, along with Chen Guangfa, to the station road police station under the jurisdiction, and transferred them to the Ximen Branch. Qiu then accused Chen of abducting his sister, and Chen accused Qiu of hiding his wife. The bureau once interrogated them, and because the statements of both parties were different and the case was disjointed, they ordered a written statement to be submitted to the Third Section of the Municipal Public Security Bureau for investigation yesterday morning.

Land Title Deed Swap: Fraud Allegation, Plaintiff Accosts Defendant, Detained by the Court 109

Wu Zhuxian, a local resident of No. 79 Xinling Village, Caishi Road, Xujiahui Road intersection, French Concession, aged 31, engaged a lawyer to file a complaint with the Criminal Division of the Court, accusing Liu Zhongxian, a local resident of No. 9 Senlin Lane, Hele Li, Jupolai Road, currently employed at the Shanghai Municipal Council’s testing department, of fraud. The complaint stated that the plaintiff and defendant were originally classmates. On April 21st of the 23rd year of the Republic (1934), the plaintiff needed to exchange a land title deed. At that time, the defendant claimed to have a good friend named Yao Shengcai who worked at the Land Bureau and could arrange the exchange for a fee of 500 yuan. The plaintiff believed him and handed over 500 silver dollars to the defendant to handle the matter. However, two years have passed without any response. Despite repeated urgings, the defendant avoided meeting him, leaving the plaintiff with no choice but to file a lawsuit. After receiving the complaint, the court repeatedly scheduled hearings, but the defendant failed to appear, hindering the progress of the trial. The court ordered a temporary suspension of the trial, pending the arrest and interrogation of the defendant Liu Zhongxian. Last Saturday, the plaintiff unexpectedly encountered Liu on the street and immediately brought him to the Second Special District Court, requesting his detention. Yesterday morning, Judge Qiu Huan-ying presided over the interrogation in the Second Criminal Court. The plaintiff recounted the previous events. The defendant Liu Zhongxian stated that the 500 yuan had been handed over to Yao Shengcai, who was no longer in Shanghai, and that he himself had not appropriated the money. After reviewing the statements, the court ordered the defendant to provide a guarantor with 1,000 yuan security or 500 yuan in cash as bail, and postponed the hearing to the 29th to locate Yao Shengcai for further questioning.

Buddhist Association Fails Twice to Take Over Longhua Temple 116

Datong News Agency reports: Since the Shanghai Buddhist Association removed the former abbot Yuanzhao from Longhua Temple due to an incident two years ago, and appointed the monk Xingkong as the new abbot to take over, it was later discovered that Yuanzhao had embezzled and sold temple property. The new abbot Xingkong then filed a lawsuit with the Shanghai Local Court. Once the lawsuit began, disputes arose repeatedly. Following the court's investigation, it was determined that Yuanzhao's embezzlement and sale of temple property was indeed true, and he was sentenced to imprisonment. From then on, the dispute subsided somewhat.

Two changes of abbot: In March of this year, the new abbot Xingkong resigned. The temple then independently elected the monk Yuanming as his successor. Now, the Shanghai Buddhist Association believes that Yuanming's succession as abbot of the temple was not the result of the Association's election and is therefore legally non-compliant. Therefore, the Association specially requested the director of the Chinese Buddhist Association, Baojing, to serve as the abbot of the temple. The Association sent personnel to take over the temple on the morning of the day before yesterday. However, the temple refused to hand over the temple, and after holding the matter until 4 p.m., they returned together without results.

Takeover fails: At 3 p.m. yesterday afternoon, the Association sent personnel to take over the temple again. In order to make it easier for the temple to comply, the chairman of the Chinese Buddhist Association, Yuanying, directors Dabei, Yuanchen, Huikai, Zhenkong, Huang Hanzhi, Wang Zhen, Guan Jiongzhi, Qu Wenliu, etc., escorted Baojing to the temple. At around 4 p.m., they arrived at the temple. Because no responsible monks were present at the temple, it was still impossible to complete the handover by 6 p.m. It was decided to return to the association first and then determine a method for taking over the temple.

This City’s Tenth Re-Registration for Group Weddings: 40 Remaining Slots, Registration Reopens Immediately 117

The ninth group wedding ceremony in this city is scheduled to be held on October 7th in the auditorium of the municipal government. The Social Affairs Bureau held registration procedures last month, and the number of applicants reached 160 couples. According to the municipal government's regulations, two ceremonies should be held. The first 100 couples registered will participate in the ninth ceremony on October 7th, and the remaining 60 couples will participate in the tenth ceremony on November 4th. Due to repeated applications from citizens to re-register, the bureau has approved 40 remaining slots and will reopen registration from today until October 15th (registration will be temporarily suspended for two days on October 6th and 7th due to the ninth group wedding). Customs Patrol Ship Intercepts Large Amount of Smuggled Goods: 120 Packages of Rayon, 4 Bags of White Sugar, Entire Ship and Cargo Escorted to Port 118

The Customs Lianxing patrol ship was patrolling the waters 300 li outside Yushan Port in Wusongkou at around 5 p.m. on the 20th when it discovered the Jinshunxing, a Ningbo fishing boat, sailing into port at high speed. Suspecting its behavior, the ship ordered it to stop for inspection. An on-site inspection revealed 120 packages of smuggled rayon transported from Lushun, each package weighing approximately 60-70 catties, for a total of 7-8,000 catties, as well as 4 bags of smuggled white sugar, each bag weighing over 100 catties, for a total of over 400 catties. The group planned to transport the goods to Yushan and then transfer them to Shanghai for sale. The ship escorted the entire ship, cargo, and six people, including the captain Wang Apin, to port. They arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning. The customs authorities consider this the first time a large amount of smuggled goods has been intercepted since the smuggling problem arose, and they are taking it very seriously. They have ordered the seized rayon and sugar to be confiscated and handed over to the government. The fishing boat used to transport smuggled goods should be detained pending disposal. The six crew members have been handed over to the Water Police for strict interrogation.

Hunan Steamboat, En Route from Tianjin to Shanghai, Female Passenger Wang Xiuchuan Jumps into the Sea, Shipowner Reports Letter, Photo, and Luggage to British Consulate, Transmitting to Municipal Government 125

Central News Agency reports: The British Taikoo Yanghang Hunan steamboat had a Chinese female passenger jump into the sea at 0:56 a.m. on September 2nd, en route from Tianjin to Shanghai. The ship immediately turned around and searched the vicinity for a long time, but her body could not be found. After investigation, it was determined that the passenger's name was Wang Xiuchuan, from Tianjin to Shanghai, approximately 30 years old, married, but her husband's name and address were unknown. A photo was found in her luggage, which is believed to be an image of the deceased herself, as well as a letter addressed to Dou Xiafei, with the words "Mr. Dou, please open" written on the envelope. The original text of the suicide note reads: "Beiping is also where I (original text as "brother") used to live. The bitterness of not being able to go is difficult to express in one or two words. I am neither happy to return north, nor willing to stay south. Thinking of the past, there was more suffering than happiness. The future is dim, with thousands of sorrows and myriad anxieties. I am disheartened and pessimistic with everything in life. My heart is broken. I am grateful for your love and affection, your warm sincerity. I can only regret meeting you too late and hope to repay you in the next life. I hope you will understand and not take it to heart. Please take care of yourself and be optimistic. I pray for this. Respectfully addressed to Mr. Xiafei for his perusal, Xiuchuan" (sealed below with a seal bearing the inscription "Jingxiu"). From this, it can be inferred that the deceased's suicide by jumping into the sea was a deliberate act born of deep sorrow. After the ship arrived in Shanghai, the shipowner immediately sent the deceased's suicide note, photo, net basket, and two boxes to the British Consulate, reporting everything. British Consul Biyuehan, after receiving the report, immediately sent the above items to the Municipal Government of this city to report the matter.

Robbery of Public Bus in Southern Shanghai, Six Bandits Arrested 127

At approximately 8 p.m. on the 7th of this month, a public bus in Southern Shanghai was driving near Luban Road and Kangqu Road when it was suddenly boarded by bandits disguised as passengers. All passengers, drivers, ticket sellers, etc., suffered losses. Since the incident occurred, the Municipal Public Security Bureau has ordered all departments to conduct strict investigations in order to apprehend and bring the perpetrators to justice. After extensive inquiries and investigations, Liu Guangjun, the captain of the Ximen Detective Division, learned that the bandits were hiding in Room 48 of the Ningxing Hotel on Ningxing Street near the Dashijie in the French Concession. After reporting to his superiors, he immediately led his team and, in cooperation with Chinese and foreign detectives from the French Police Department, rushed to the scene at 6 a.m. yesterday, where they arrested six bandits: Sun Zhiliang, Jin Miaoxing, Hu Yifei (alias Ding Hongcai), Qi Yucai, Cai Yongsheng, and Song Quanqing. They were taken to the police station for temporary detention, pending their transfer to the Second Special District Court by the Municipal Public Security Bureau for interrogation and legal proceedings.

Another reporting investigator reported that the Detective Division of the West Dou Public Security Sub-bureau received a confidential tip at 6 a.m. yesterday that bandits were hiding in Rooms 48 and 49 of the Ningxing Hotel at No. 479, Min Tini Yin Road, Aiduya Road, French Concession. The team dispatched detectives and requested assistance from the special unit of the French Police Department, sending Chinese and foreign detectives to Room 48 of the Ningxing Hotel, where they arrested Jin Miaoxing (36 years old), a local resident, and Ding Hongfan, also known as Wu Yifei (25 years old, a ticket collector at the Xinguang Theater). They arrested Qi Yuelin (22 years old), a Shandong native, and Wang Longdi (22 years old), a prostitute from Huzhou, in Room 49. However, no handguns or weapons were found during a search of the two rooms. They were taken back to the police station. It was discovered that Jin Miao had previously been sentenced to six years' imprisonment by the First Special District Court for a theft case and was temporarily detained. They were then transferred to the First Criminal Court of the Second Special Court, where Judge Zhang Chaozuo presided over the hearing. Fei Xizhen, the lawyer of the police department, explained the case and requested a postponement. The investigator of the Ximen Public Security Sub-bureau reported that the defendants were related to a robbery case on Luban Road and that the transfer documents could not be processed in time, requesting a postponement. He also stated that three more people had been apprehended since the defendants were arrested and were currently at the police station. After reviewing the report, the court questioned the defendants. It was determined that the fourth defendant, Wang Longdi, was a prostitute who had met Qi Yuelin in the Dashijie the night before and shared a room with him, and was not significantly related to the case. Wang Longdi was ordered to provide a suitable guarantor, and those without guarantors were detained. The remaining defendants were remanded in custody and the hearing was postponed to the afternoon of the 25th.

Taxpayers Association Letters Shanghai Municipal Council, Requests Compassionate Aid for Shen Ruting 128

The Shanghai Public Concession Taxpayers Association yesterday sent a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Council, stating: To whom it may concern, we have received a letter from the Shaoxing Seven Counties Shanghai Fellow-Provincials Association, stating that member Shen Ruting reported in his letter that he entered the Fourth Ma Road Fire Brigade at the age of 28, Western name Shen Ating, also known as Tu Kang, number 59, and was later transferred to the Yangshupu Fire Brigade, where he has served until the age of 51. He has continued his firefighting work for over 20 years. Whenever there is a fire, he bravely goes forward without any mistakes. On January 20th of this year, the electric light factory on Yangshupu Road, Lan Road, suddenly reported a fire. Ruting, as his duty demanded, immediately went to extinguish it. Unexpectedly, the current overflowed, and he was severely injured. Although he received treatment and managed to survive, his limbs are bent, and his face is scorched. He has become disabled. The Westerners at the association, considering him a disabled employee who cannot continue to work, have only agreed to subsidize his original salary for one and a half years before terminating his employment. Thinking of the long days ahead, and a family of old and young to feed, how can he survive on such a small subsidy? He earnestly requests the authorities to provide compassionate aid and allow him to receive his original salary for five years, along with all his savings over the years, paid in one lump sum, to support him for the rest of his years. He would be immensely grateful. Upon investigation, Shen Ruting was disabled in the line of duty, a truly pitiful situation. The requested five years of salary is not excessive. Attached is a copy of the letter for your reference. Accordingly, we request the council to uphold justice and appeal on his behalf. It is hoped that you will investigate, etc. It has come to our attention that Shen Ruting is so brave, loyal to his duties, and disabled in the line of duty. The aid he receives is only one and a half years of his original salary. Compared to recent retirees, who have served for fewer years than Shen, the benefits they receive are many times greater in proportion. The disparity is obvious. We request that the council grant him the satisfaction he desires, as an encouragement, and advise that from now on, the council should treat its employees equally, regardless of nationality. Although there may be differences in salaries, such as pensions, savings, etc., the methods should be uniform. Do not let disparities permanently exist, in order to show the permanence of justice and the elimination of bias. Based on the above, we are sending this letter, hoping that you will investigate, and in addition to providing Shen Ruting with compassionate aid, readjust the retirement procedures for council members, for your attention. Addressed to Secretary-General of Shanghai Public Concession Municipal Council.

Minfeng Company: Domestic Cigarette Paper Production and Sales Statistics After Creating Cigarette Paper 133

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, cigarettes are one of the most consumed items in our country. For years, the paper used to manufacture cigarettes has relied on imports, resulting in significant leakage of funds. Since Zhu Meixian and Jin Runxiang of Minfeng Paper Company started creating this cigarette paper, they have purchased machinery and received exclusive manufacturing rights from the Ministry of Industry. They started shipping products several months ago, and their quality is comparable to imported goods, with sales becoming popular domestically. It is said that Minfeng originally ordered two sets of cigarette paper machines. However, since this machine was a new invention in the country, for the sake of caution, only one set was shipped first. Each machine can produce 1,250 rolls per day, totaling 420,000 rolls per year. The two machines can produce a total of 840,000 rolls per year. Compared with the domestic demand at the time, the supply and demand were corresponding. However, in recent years, the market has been depressed, and various places have vigorously promoted the New Life Movement, causing people to quit smoking cigarettes, resulting in a step-by-step reduction in cigarette sales. According to the statistics of the Cigarette Tax Bureau, in the first half of this year, the actual number of cigarettes manufactured by various cigarette factories in the country was 354,178 boxes for foreign-owned factories and 199,558 boxes for Chinese-owned factories. Each box uses one roll of cigarette paper. Based on this calculation, excluding foreign-owned cigarette factories, only 199,558 rolls of paper are used, and only 399,116 rolls of cigarette paper are needed for the whole year. Among them, a part is still inevitably using foreign goods. Therefore, Minfeng's current production capacity of one machine has an excess of supply over demand. Therefore, Minfeng is hesitant about whether the other set of machines that has been ordered but not yet arrived should still be shipped to China. In fact, cigarettes are a consumable, and it is a very good phenomenon that Chinese people can gradually reduce smoking. It cannot be said that it is not an achievement of the New Life Movement.

Tongyi Trust Company: Lawsuits Consolidated for Trial; Where are the 180,000 Savings Deposits? The Court Believes a Thorough Investigation is Necessary 134

Since Tongyi Trust Company went bankrupt on June 15th and the director and general manager, Huang Suchu, quietly left Shanghai, depositors have filed lawsuits against the company's entire board of directors and supervisors in the First Special District Local Court. Some have already had preliminary trials and judgments, some are still in trial, and some are just beginning to file lawsuits. Yesterday afternoon, the court continued to hear the case jointly filed by Lu Tangcha, Ying Shugui, and Wang Meiqing against the company's directors and supervisors for violating the Company Law. Since depositors Zhang Peiyan and Xu Xiangsun also sued the company's directors and supervisors for violating the Company Law, Judge Ye Shengchao announced after the hearing that the cases would be consolidated for trial to save time. He then ordered the plaintiffs to present evidence of their deposits for review. Among them, Lu, Ying, and Wang had deposited public debt certificates, requesting a judgment ordering repayment of more than 176,000 yuan. Zhang Peiyan's was a current deposit, plus interest, totaling more than 36,500 yuan. Xu Xiangsun was representing the organization he led and deposited more than 2,700 yuan of savings funds into the company's savings department. The lawyers representing the plaintiffs often argued that since the defendants were the directors and supervisors executing the company's business, they should be responsible for the company's actions. For example, when the company applied for registration, it stated that the capital was 2.5 million, but now it is found that the actual amount received was only 1.36 million. There was no profit in the business, but the depositors' money was transferred to distribute dividends to shareholders. All of these are violations of the Company Law. When operating savings, they should first register according to the law. The company had never complied with the Savings Bank Law to apply for registration, and requested an investigation. However, only Xu Jixun, Zhou Shouliang, Guo Yushang, and Fu Zhuyin, along with defense lawyer Xu Shihao, appeared in court. The rest, Huang Suchu, Liu Fangyuan, Liu Rensan, Neng Muzhai, and Wu Jingwen, were all in hiding and did not appear. Jiang Liuzhi still claimed illness, and a lawyer represented him in court. Judge Ye reviewed the company's balance sheet for 1935 and found that more than 180,000 yuan of savings deposits had been deposited in other banks and businesses. He questioned Xu, Zhou, Guo, and Fu about the numbers of other banks and businesses. Xu and others all said that they were not the directors who executed the business, and they never inquired about the internal affairs of the company. Although it was recorded in the table, they had never seen the detailed accounts, so they did not know. Judge Ye believed that it was necessary to thoroughly investigate the whereabouts of more than 180,000 yuan of deposits, so he adjourned the hearing to the afternoon of the 25th of this month for further questioning.

Kuang Zhongmou and Wife's Debt Lawsuit: Huge Amount of Rent Seized; Totaling More Than 19,000 Yuan; Approved by the Court for Execution 142

Kuang Zhongmou, the owner of the Penglai Market and a wealthy merchant from Liangxi, and his elderly wife, Kuang Zeng, are both over fifty years old. Kuang Zeng once used hundreds of yuan accumulated from her hard work to invest in Kuang's business when he was still poor. Later, he became wealthy, and they settled as 20,000 yuan, and Kuang issued a passbook to his wife. To date, the principal and interest have reached more than 30,000 yuan. After the couple fell out, Kuang Zeng filed a lawsuit in the Local Court. After three trials, the final judgment was that Kuang should return the money. Not long ago, Kuang hired lawyer Zhang Shijian and others to request a retrial, which also failed. The case is now under execution. However, Kuang has never paid. The lawyer representing Kuang Zeng found that the 34 stores in the Penglai Market had originally paid a monthly rent of 20 yuan per room. Later, Kuang increased the rent by 5 yuan, which was met with dissatisfaction from the public. The tenants organized a tenant union and deposited the monthly rent in the Shanghai Bank, totaling more than 28 months, amounting to 680 yuan in national currency per month, totaling more than 22,000 yuan including interest. They requested the court to withdraw the money from the bank for execution. The court has approved it. However, the tenants only agreed to pay the original amount of 19,040 yuan. The interest should still belong to the tenants. Now that Kuang Zhongmou's money has been withdrawn, he is shouting.

Chen Jingchu and He Chengfu: Dispute Over Daughter Continues; Neither Will Relinquish Temporary Adoption; The Case Awaits Transfer to the Local Court 143

Chen Jingchu, a native of Yancheng who is now an inspector at the Shanghai Education Bureau, had his wife, Wu, die of illness on July 8th last year. She left behind three children, two boys and one girl. He adopted his four-year-old daughter, Xiaofeng, to his friend He Chengfu, the dean of studies at Minli Women's High School and a professor at Qingxin Women's School, and his wife, He Qiu. Recently, Chen suddenly wanted to take back the girl. Negotiations were ineffective. Chen then filed a complaint with the French Concession Police Department, accusing the He couple of luring the child. After the police department sent investigator Zhou Bingcheng to summon the He couple for questioning, the police department's lawyer filed a public prosecution with the Second Special District Court in accordance with Article 241 of the Criminal Law. Under the trial of Judge Zhang Chaozuo, he advised both parties to reconcile. However, both parties refused to give in, especially on the matter of compensation. Chen firmly refused, resulting in the breakdown of the reconciliation. Both parties wanted to take the child. The court ruled that the jurisdiction of the case was wrong and ordered the transfer to the Shanghai Local Court for handling. The girl was sent to a daycare center, and both parties were ordered to pay 50 yuan to the case. When the Shanghai Local Court determined who would take back the child, the report stated that whoever would take them back would. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Zhang of the Second Special Court issued summonses to Chen Jingchu and He Chengfu to appear in court. He opened a special criminal court and informed both parties that the girl, Xiaofeng, was originally ordered by the court to be sent to a daycare center for care. Because the center's regulations stipulated that there were day and night classes, children in the daytime were aged two to four, and children at night were aged six months and above. Xiaofeng was already four years old and could not be kept in accordance with the regulations. So today they summoned both of you to see if you could compromise and let one party temporarily adopt the child, because the Guangci Hospital is a charitable institution and cannot keep the child in the hospital for a long time. Chen Jingchu said that he requested permission to seek security and that the child should be temporarily adopted by a third party, the child's maternal grandmother. He Chengfu said that the child had been with his family for fourteen months and was now suffering in the hospital. Moreover, the third party, the maternal grandmother, mentioned by Chen lived with Chen and was supported by Chen, so he could not let her take her away. He requested that the child still be taken back and raised by the people. The court reviewed the statements and found that both parties still refused to give in, so it ordered that the child be temporarily kept in Guangci Hospital and that the case be transferred to the Shanghai Local Court for handling.

Special District Rickshaw Pullers Petition to Cancel Reduction of Vehicles; Request to Cancel the Agreement to Reduce Vehicles; and Reorganize the Mutual Aid Association and Vehicle Committee 144

After the Municipal Council passed the reduction of 500 public rickshaws to 9,500 by March 1st of next year, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Mutual Aid Association, Chinese directors, rickshaw merchants, and rickshaw pullers have expressed their opposition one after another. Due to the past quota registration of rickshaw pullers by the Municipal Council, more than 20,000 rickshaw pullers in the Special District have lost their jobs. Now, without considering the public, they want to reduce the number of vehicles, which will increase the number of unemployed rickshaw pullers by more than a thousand. Therefore, at 10:00 a.m. yesterday, more than 50 representatives, including Cang Gongwen, He Wushan, Xu Zhulin, Zhu Fengxiang, Zhu Richang, Bian Weidong, and Xing Decai, prepared documents and petitioned the Municipal Council, the board of directors, the general office, the Chinese directors, and taxpayers, requesting: (1) Cancel the agreement to reduce vehicles; (2) Reorganize the Mutual Aid Association and Vehicle Committee; (3) Register rickshaw pullers for a long time without restrictions. It is said that the rickshaw merchants also plan to petition various parties in the coming days.

Robbery on Qu Zhenren Road 145

At 7:30 p.m. last night, three robbers wearing blue-black short coats suddenly came to Baokang Cigarette and Paper Store at No. 813 Qu Zhenren Road at the intersection of Xinqiao Road in Nanshi. The apprentice of the store happened to open the iron gate to go out for shopping. The robbers took the opportunity to rush in, speaking in Shanghai dialect, and showed two handguns, imprisoning them from moving. They robbed a total of more than 50 yuan in banknotes and corner tickets from the account desk and fled south without a trace. Wu Baoyi, the owner of the store, reported the case to the police station in charge for investigation.

"Nosey" and "Blessings Collection" to be Published 146

The first Chinese humorous comic "Nosey" by Huang Yao, has already published two volumes and sold well at home and abroad, reaching more than 20,000 copies. It has won high praise from the United States, Germany, England, Japan, and other countries, who believe that "it collects the humorous points of today's Chinese people, displays the rich Chinese jokes, and introduces China's unique humor, which is truly passed into the eyes and reflected in the brain, and can be recalled and laughed at anytime. Not only is it deeply interesting, but it also contains subtle satire. Its style is unique in the international comic book world. It uses very simple lines to draw very lively movements and delicate expressions, which is even more rare. The protagonist's half-nose face and body are well-organized, and it is extremely easy to imitate, so children like to imitate it and recognize Nosey as a representative of Chinese humor." The first volume has been published three times, and the second volume has been published twice. Both are distributed by China Bookstore Company on Fuzhou Road in this city. The third volume has now been collected with excellent masterpieces, and there is also a "Blessings Collection", which contains single-panel satirical paintings, purely performed by Nosey, still taking a humorous tone, mocking all social figures. The cover is printed in four colors and is beautiful. The price is still set at 15 cents, which has been compiled and will be published soon.

Currently, the book is broadcast daily on Li Xiede Radio (frequency 940) by Chinese and English teachers and is very popular among the general audience. The book sells for 80 cents per copy. New Plans for Friends Beer 149

Shanghai Brewery Company has been launching countless plans for Friends Beer recently, making it popular far and wide and well-known. Letter 150

We have reviewed a news item published in your newspaper on the 10th of this month about a robbery near Qimei Road in which passengers in a car were robbed and the driver was shot. It does not conform to the facts and should be corrected as follows: (1) The portion of the passengers being robbed of more than 100 yuan in cash. On the evening of the 9th of this month at about 9:00 p.m., the victim, Zhang Baogen, hired a Xiang Sheng taxi to Qimei Road. He was robbed by bandits and lost six yuan and three cents in banknotes and a gold ring. (2) The portion of the car driver, Lin Haigen, being shot in the right arm. At that time, the car driver, Lin Haigen, wanted to rush forward, so he was shot at the car window by the bandits, but he was not hit. Only the glass was broken, and the glass shards hit the driver's right arm, causing only minor injuries. In addition to sending separate letters, we hereby request you to check and correct it. Respectfully to Shen Bao Newspaper, Shanghai Public Security Bureau, September 22nd.

Weather Report 151

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 p.m. yesterday stated that the sky around Shandong is cloudy and sunny, with southwest to northwest winds. The weather in the Yellow River basin is changing from cloudy to overcast, with north to east winds. The upper and middle reaches of the Yangtze River are clear and calm and without direction. The lower reaches of the Yangtze River, the East China Sea, and Taiwan all have morning fog, and southeast to northeast winds. The hurricane is obviously passing Saipan northward to the northwest. Its center reached within 120 miles of 20 degrees north latitude and 144 degrees east longitude at noon. The wind force is unknown. Also, within 24 hours before 3:00 p.m. yesterday, the temperature in this port was 92.1 degrees at its highest and 62.2 degrees at its lowest. On the same day last year, the highest was 82.4 and the lowest was 61.9.

Fictitious Film Company Scams Guarantee Money; Jobless Rush to Register; Han Liansheng Accused of Fraud 152

Han Liansheng (also known as Han Lisheng), a native of Zhenjiang, being in dire straits, rented a spare room at No. 1102, Avenue Edward VII, last month. He put up a sign for the "Gangxing Film Company" and advertised, claiming the company needed staff and trainee actors with certain monthly salaries. This attracted many unemployed people to register. Han seized the opportunity to extort money, setting the amount of the guarantee deposit based on the applicant's situation, ranging from five to thirty yuan. Within a month, the amount of money swindled was considerable. Recently, victims Sun Zhibei, Sun Lin, Qiu Xijin, Wang Pingji, Sun Zhiying, Hua Rongrong, Wu Xianqing, etc., discovered the scam and reported it to the Chengdu Road Police Station. The police dispatched officers and arrested Han the day before yesterday. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the First Special District Local Court, where Judge Zhan Liang conducted a preliminary hearing. Police lawyer Jiang Baolian charged Han with fraud, requesting severe punishment according to the law. Each victim was brought to court to testify about their experience of being deceived and the amount of money lost. When questioned, Han confessed to setting up a fictitious film company to fraudulently obtain guarantee deposits. Judge Zhan, after a clear investigation, ordered the defendant to be detained pending sentencing next week.

Shen Bao National Goods Special

National Goods Movement: Echoes from Interviewers 154

Quite by chance, we were given the opportunity to be selected as national goods movement interviewers. However, in terms of using and promoting national goods, this did not just start today.

From today onwards, we will take this iron burden completely onto our own shoulders, and unflinchingly embark on this arduous journey; the responsibility is significant, yet what we feel in our hearts is lightness and joy.

The slogan "Promote National Goods" is perhaps shouted loudly even by three-year-olds. In fact, alarming customs import statistics can often be found in newspapers, and are undeniable. Therefore, the current work of the national goods movement cannot focus solely on shouting slogans; it should be more practical, more in-depth, and grounded in reality, so that everyone has the good concept of "must use national goods."

We have been selected to be the outposts bearing this practical work. How could we not feel both ashamed and honored! Our work has already begun for a week.

In this short week, we have visited nearly twenty well-known national goods factories in this city. Although due to the urgency of time, there have not been more opportunities for discussion, under the guidance of national goods movement pioneers and the detailed instructions of enthusiastic leaders of various national goods factories, coupled with what we have gained from on-site observation, one cannot help but deeply believe that our national goods are increasingly refined. Whether in terms of quality or form, they can more than replace foreign goods.

1. Raw materials and machinery: If there are national goods available, they are invariably used, and there are frequent inventions and imitations (such as the silk of the Yabu Er Electrical Factory, the filter tanks of the Tianchu MSG Factory, the machinery of the Yaguang Bakelite Factory, the raw materials for the Xin Ya Pharmaceutical Airplane Brand Pencils, and the steel skin of the Dahua Iron Factory, etc.).

2. Manufacturing procedures are highly economical and hygienic (such as the success of the Zhongfa Pharmacy in imitating foreign medicines using Chinese methods, and the rationalized management of the Wuzhou Pharmacy).

3. Daily necessities are all beautiful, economical, and durable (such as the fabrics of the Xin Xin Weaving Factory, the woolens of the Zhanghua Weaving Factory, the silks of the Meiya Silk Weaving Factory, the cotton textiles of the Sanyou Industrial Society, the Shidai Shuang Cream of the China Chemical Industrial Society, the Qiandou Brand Tooth Powder of the Family Industrial Society, and various fans of the Huasheng Electrical Factory, etc.).

4. Sales are flourishing and reaching foreign countries (the business of the China National Goods Company is quite considerable. Wuhe cotton毛衫sweaters are selling well in Russia and India. The Kangyuan Canning Factory and Tianchu MSG sell 50-60% to the UK and the US. The products of Meiya, Yongxing, and the China Enamel Factory are mostly sold to Southeast Asia, Singapore, etc.).

These are all practical examples. No matter how eloquent one may be, how can one deny the facts? Having seen these facts, what more sufficient reasons can we have to deny the advantages of national goods, and to bear to be promoters of foreign goods, intentionally or unintentionally!

The factory visits of the past few days have given us rich knowledge and enhanced our love for national goods. We will more resolutely vow to be users of national goods.

In a few days, we will take our confidence in and love for national goods deep into the streets and alleys, to gain the confidence of general housewives and arouse their enthusiasm for using national goods.

Our knowledge is shallow, our experience is insufficient, and it is almost an overestimation of our abilities to attempt this work, but we believe that we will not shy away from difficulties, and we will work patiently to make the housewives our close friends. Between us, we will talk about everything from household matters to the comparison between national goods and foreign goods, as loving and using national goods is a citizen's natural duty. To achieve our goal of faithfully serving families and completing the important mission we have been entrusted with.

Finally, we have inexpressible gratitude for the encouragement given by the media, the enthusiastic guidance of national goods leaders, and the supervision of people from all walks of life. We can only offer our efforts in our work as a salute!

Interviewers: Xu Chengqing, Xu Songzi, Chen Yingfen, Lin Wen, Shen Wenxian

Writer: Xu Songzi

Three days after September 18th

A Word of Contribution

National Goods Cuisine 155

— Yang An

On one occasion, Mr. Lin Kanghou, Mr. Huang Renzhi, and other gentlemen gathered for dinner with gentlemen from the national goods community. Mr. Lin lamented the extravagance of banquets, believing that in this time of national crisis and the era of promoting a new lifestyle, this kind of practice should be corrected to create a new innovation for the people. Therefore, he advocated that in the future, our banquets should promote a kind of national goods cuisine to be promoted domestically as a standard. Mr. Huang was the first to agree, and everyone unanimously praised and expressed their sympathy. National goods cuisine is also called Five Lakes Four Seas cuisine, with four dishes and five bowls. The five bowls consist of four main dishes and one soup. It is both simple and practical, with the price determined by the quality of the materials. The high-end costs five yuan, the mid-range three yuan, and the low-end one or two yuan, with the total cost per person not exceeding five jiao. All the ingredients and drinks used are domestically produced, without shark fin or abalone. The needs of a feast are not costly, and the time spent can be completed in twenty or thirty minutes. This is truly worth promoting and is also worthy of being implemented. In particular, the national goods community should take the lead to popularize it in companies, shops, and factories. The effect will be swift and influential. I hope that the whole country will consider it and put it into practice! Chinese people, should know what time it is today! The national crisis is so serious, and the national situation is so degraded that it is not enough to be frugal to deal with others, and it is not enough to survive today without reducing consumption. At present, our own situation can only be to work hard to produce and restrain enjoyment. It's good to produce one point more, and it's good to enjoy a little less. Without mass production, it is not enough to be self-sufficient, and without careful enjoyment, it is not enough to establish a life and live in peace. Mr. Lu Zuofu hung a slogan in the Minsheng Company: "Produce boldly, enjoy carefully." The words are sincere and meaningful and are the words of a man of good conscience. Our advocacy of national goods cuisine is also a means of carefully enjoying in order to save the country from its plight. My patriotic compatriots, may they also know how to rise up!

"Autumn" and National Goods 156

— Xuan Wan

Yingfen, Lin Wen, Shen Wenxian Writer: Xu Songzi "September 18th" Three Days Later

Time flies like an arrow, and the autumn season of the Municipal National Goods Year is quickly presenting itself before us again. The rustling autumn wind has already moved the various companies and commercial venues, with high-hanging banners proclaiming "Autumn Great Sale." Dazzling advertisements are already exerting their power, touching our eyes. It seems to be telling us very clearly – "Autumn has arrived."

Based on past experience, facts also tell us that "autumn" is a major period of climatic change in the year, and people's lives therefore urgently need to purchase all kinds of autumn supplies. Similarly, the dumping of foreign goods is precisely the most active opportunity. At this time, the influx of imported goods into our markets will again compete for novelty and difference to win their customers. What's more, the Mid-Autumn Festival is just around the corner. We can already see those batches of "foreign goods promoters" about to buy large quantities of imported cigarettes, alcohol, candies, biscuits, and canned foods! To use as gifts and embellish this great season. Here, I want to cry out loudly, hoping that Chinese people will no longer make the mistakes of the past, and no longer make the mistake of being a manufacturer of huge trade deficits in a confused state.

Moreover, at present, the economic crisis of the nation is already serious to this point. The dumping of foreign goods has already reached the stage of swallowing up the vitality of our entire nation, and we can no longer have illusions about "material enjoyment." This time, the Fifth National Goods Commercial Venue of Nine Factories is opening on the fifth anniversary of September 18th, using the promotion of national goods to express not forgetting the national crisis. This has great significance. I hope that every patriotic compatriot will promote and cherish it.

Finally, I also want to say that when the autumn season has come again in the City National Goods Year, the shuttle of time has quickly rolled away three-quarters of its days. We must always examine ourselves, regarding the achievements of the past eight months of this year, how does it compare to last year? Then, the production and sales of national goods have undoubtedly made very significant progress in recent times, especially in penetrating the interior and making great efforts to promote sales, there has been great success. Although what hinders us and requires greater efforts in the future still remains the development of transportation construction and the solution of the smuggling problem, etc. In short, the future of national goods is bright and promising, as long as we all work together, we will definitely develop to a higher and newer stage.

Sports News

Our World Games Soccer Team's Performance in London: Performance Praised for Excellence 158

London Reuters News: The Chinese football team's match against the Corinthians team featured seven international amateur players. The Chinese team's performance was clear and beautiful. After the two teams stood against each other, the national anthems of both countries were played simultaneously. Before the music had even finished, the Chinese team had already opened the scoring. The Chinese team's victory in this goal, in terms of cooperation, had surprising ingenuity, thus reminding people of why the English and Chinese teams in Berlin were so unusually close and tense.

The first goal was scored in the twentieth minute, the center forward scoring with admirable composure. Its beauty had not been seen in years. The Chinese players shoot very well, and the technique of passing the ball is also very wonderful.

Corinthians won 3-2 but had exhausted their efforts. Huang Jiliang's goalkeeping was also unexpectedly good. The Chinese team scorers were Feng Jingxiang and Li Huitang.

The Chinese team adopted the British style of attack, with the center back far behind, and the center forward advancing straight ahead. In the middle of the second half, the situation declined slightly. Before the end of the war, they launched a strong counterattack, which was a pity to be unsuccessful.

Cai Wenli was the best fullback on the field. The Chinese team's goalkeeping performance has not been surpassed in the Haibolay this season.

Overview of Japanese Schools in Shanghai (5) 179

— Special Report by This Newspaper: Investigation by Hu Zuyin

Six, Children's Training

Ten minutes before class every morning, all teachers and children line up in the sports field. First, raise the national flag to the sound of the national anthem, and then perform a remote worship ceremony to the Japanese Emperor facing south. At this time, the principal and the teacher on duty may give speeches on occasional matters and other moral education matters. On Army and Navy Memorial Day, National Foundation Day, or other memorial days, staff members also give speeches or invite celebrities to give speeches. For the respected figures in Japanese history, such as General Nogi, Marshal Togo, and the Forty-Seven Loyal Retainers, lectures are also given at the prescribed times.

Teachers must carefully observe the children's personality, academic performance, physical condition, and the children's strengths and weaknesses, and must record them in the school register for reference in rewards or corrections. Children with excellent character and learning or those who study diligently are also commended. If a child does something particularly good or virtuous, the principal will convene all the children to the auditorium to announce the matter to the public for instruction. Admonishment and punishment will also be used when necessary.

Teachers also pay attention to children's service and labor training. Students in the sixth grade and above can elect representatives to assist the teacher on duty in handling the work of maintaining school discipline and hygiene. From the second grade, each grade is set up with one head and one deputy grade leader to assist in the implementation of autonomous training. The planting of the school garden and the maintenance of poultry are undertaken by students. The cleaning and tidying of the classroom are carried out by the on-duty students in rotation. In addition, the school often rewards students for diligence and thrift; and holds a thrift week to make children consciously aware of the meaning and methods of diligence and thrift and savings.

There are many drills for emergency gathering training in the school, and punctuality training is also encouraged. Children often go to participate in various shrines, festival days, and festival ceremonies. If a classmate dies or a classmate's parent dies, all the children in the grade will hold a memorial service to express their farewell. For the death or departure of a teacher, all students in the school will hold a memorial service or go to the wharf to see them off, expressing their respect. In the practical training of etiquette, attention is paid to the correctness of posture and the avoidance of rude language and actions. Usually, children's clothing and etiquette are carefully guided.

Seven, Children's Nurturing

Regarding the policy of nurturing children, the Japanese school authorities believe that attention should be paid to the individual physical constitution of children, so that children are consciously aware of the value of health care, and can further seek help in growth and development, and improve the path to health, in order to cultivate strong bodies and minds. Japanese schools are very concerned about the physical and mental health and hygiene of children, and believe that the improvement of children's physical and mental health is a major goal of their school. The work they carry out in nurturing is now described in two aspects, positive and negative.

On the positive side, there are school-wide exercises every morning and after lunch, implementing national gymnastics. The normal daily gymnastics are implemented according to the revised outline of the Ministry of Education. Extracurricular sports are held once or twice a week, and children participate freely. Sports meets are held once every semester to cultivate the spirit of sports and advancement in children. School excursions are held regularly; small excursions are held once a month, and large excursions are held once every semester, with the aim of training children's bodies.

A health week is held once every autumn; various health activities are actively implemented with the sports association as the center. In summer, the school grounds are also open, and children can still come to school to exercise. Students who are willing to participate in swimming can practice swimming in the summer after a physical examination. There are also martial arts clubs at ordinary times, held once every semester, to cultivate children's wrestling and judo skills. A martial arts tournament is held at the end of each semester to train children's physique and develop children's fortitude, decisiveness, endurance, courage, and progressive virtues. In severe cold or hot weather, there is often a week of kendo practice to cultivate children's perseverance.

On the negative side, each school holds a regular physical examination once every spring, and the results of the examination are recorded in detail on the physical examination form. Regarding oral hygiene, such as: tooth decay, tonsils, etc., there is a separate examination form to notify the children's parents, and introduce appropriate and responsible doctors, so that parents can take their children to seek treatment. In May and January of each year, when necessary, the school may hold temporary physical examinations. After examining the body, appropriate arrangements are made for changing the children's seats and changing the seats.

Usually, a cleaning inspection is held once a week, and attention is paid to the cleanliness of the students' desks, chairs, and clothing in each grade. The cleaning work of each classroom every day is the responsibility of the on-duty students; a major cleaning is held once at the beginning and end of each semester. Every year before the rainy season, before the summer vacation, and during the epidemic of infectious diseases, school doctors and specialized doctors are specially invited to the school to give lectures to students on hygiene matters. The third week of each month is designated as hygiene week, paying special attention to whether students have taken a bath; the cleanliness of their hair, neck, and fingernails, and whether they have developed the habit of not spitting everywhere.

Finance: Buyers Seem Eager; Standard Gold Recovers Eighty Cents 180

Although the gold market was weak and not much yesterday, buyers were more eager. The market was stable as soon as it opened, and the trend was stronger in the middle, but it was erratic. In the end, it was still stable. In the early morning, the overseas silver market saw a slight decrease in London and no change in the U.S., the forward silver price in Monterey did not move, and the exchange rate decreased slightly. The price of raw gold in London fell by half a penny. The central bank's listing revealed that the English and American markets were flat, and the customs gold unit did not move. The standard gold price was listed at 1116 yuan and eighty cents. Over-the-counter pre-trading opened down to within 23 yuan. Hengyudemaoyong took advantage of the low prices to enter the market, and the morning opening was slightly higher. After opening, there was a lack of supply, and buyers moved one after another. The Hong Kong and Shanghai Banking Corporation's listing revealed that the English and American markets were flat. The price gradually rose. The silver balance tax revealed a decrease of half a cent. After entering the market, there was more outflow of sales, and the price fell again. At noon, the price was stable because there was still maintenance to take advantage of the low prices. The market was stable and slightly lower in the afternoon, but the selling pressure was limited. Big players took advantage of the situation to buy, and transactions were scarce. The table was relatively dry. Finally, it gradually pulled up, and the prices of silver ingots were flat twice. The result tended to be stable. The swap was initially posted by the multilateral side at 2 yuan and ninety cents. The daily market situation is recorded below:

The morning opening was 1123 yuan and thirty cents, a slight increase of one cent compared to the previous close. Shendayongfutai, Dadecheng, Fuxingyong, and others submitted notes one after another. The Hong Kong and Shanghai Banking Corporation's listing revealed that the English and American markets were flat, gradually rising to 4 yuan and 1 cent. The silver balance tax revealed a decrease of half a cent. Shengyuanyongchengdadadecheng supplied and sold, falling to 3 yuan and 2 cents. Dingkangqiafengyong took advantage of the low prices to maintain, and the noon close was 1123 yuan and a half.

The afternoon market opened at 1113 yuan and seven cents. Yuanmaoyong advanced and then retreated. Retail investors and Shendayong also sold, falling to yuan and four cents. Dadecheng Fuxingyong Qingfayong Huixiang Dafeng Heng bought in bulk, gradually rising until the close was 1124 yuan.

The closing price was based on the central bank's standard gold price, which was listed at 1116 yuan and eighty cents. In terms of the closing price, it was about 10 yuan higher. The registration for this month was 1118 yuan, 1121 yuan for October, and 1124 yuan for November. The replenishment in the morning was 1118 yuan. The spot market was stable, and the bare red was sold at an additional 11 yuan and a half by Dadecheng for 70 taels, and Dafengheng sold 70 taels. The purchase price was an additional 7 yuan, and the Tianjin goods were an additional 9 yuan and a half, with no opponents. The swap was 2 yuan and ninety cents posted by Hengyu to Yuanmaoyong for 7 notes. 35 October notes were transferred from Wanxing to Dadecheng, priced at yuan.

The trading in the market was average. In summary, Shendayong, Dadecheng, Futaiyong, Fuxingyong, Qiafengyong, Jiuyong, Dademaoyong, Dafenghengqingfayong, Hengyu Huixiang and others were on the buying side, while Shengyuanyong, Qianchangxiangcheng, Daxingfeng and others were on the selling side. Dadecheng and Shendayong advanced and then retreated, while Yuanmaoyong first went out and then came in.

The daily market situation was stable. The morning opening was 1123 yuan and thirty cents, and the closing was 1124 yuan. The highest price was 1124 yuan and 1 cent, and the lowest price was 1123 yuan and 2 cents, a difference of 9 cents. The result was a recovery of 8 cents compared to the previous close. There are still 595 notes remaining in this month, a total of 8 long parties and 5 short parties. There are still 1218 October notes remaining, a total of 11 long parties and 12 short parties. There are a total of 7259 November chips, with 28 bulls and 40 bears. The total number of transactions was 483 notes in the pre-market and 322 notes in the post-market.

Securities: Spot Goods Show Obvious Outflow, Unified B Bonds Plunge 80 Cents 182

Yesterday, the bond market of the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange was shocked by the changes in the political situation. The situation in Hankou caused a surge of spot goods onto the market. Although there were no major storms in the market, the overall trend was downward throughout the day, a rare level of activity in recent weeks. Large investors were selling near-term bonds, indicating they possessed spot goods, suggesting a continued small decline is likely. Yesterday's trading saw heavy selling of the 10th and 54th issues during the morning opening, while the 4th and 38th issues saw some buying, rebounding slightly by 1.5 to 3.5 cents. In the second session, retail investors, recognizing the difficulty of the market to fall repeatedly, immediately engaged in short covering, stabilizing the market slightly. Type E remained unchanged, Type C was slightly better by 5 cents, while other issues such as the 11th and 14th continued to be sold off, falling by 5 cents to 1 or 2 cents. The afternoon opening saw selling of the 5th, 10th, and 35th issues, mostly of the current month, widely understood as spot goods flowing out. The downward trend was irreversible, and the closing price fell again by 5 cents to 1 or 2.5 cents, showing a weakened state and a possible continued decline. With only two days left in the month, selling pressure increased, and a short squeeze may be unavoidable. The final market prices saw Type B fall the most, by 80 cents, and Type E fall the least, by 40 cents. 96 also fell by 2-3 cents. The total trading volume was 8,595,000 yuan. Marked Yarn Weak in the Morning, Up in the Afternoon

The marked yarn market opened weak in the morning due to continued declines in American cotton. With the current month's yarn delivery approaching, sentiment was loose, and near-term contracts fell 6-7 cents. In the second session, the current month's momentum was quite weak, almost breaking the 9 yuan mark. Subsequently, spot yarn merchants, noting that the price was about 2 yuan lower than spot yarn, withdrew 1,000 bales of warehouse receipts for White Flying Fish, Globe, Heavenly Official, and Awake Lion yarns, raising prices. Far-term contracts were pulled upward, but large firms like Changfeng, Dachang, and Tongji came to sell, creating heavy pressure. However, the general industry collectively absorbed the supply, with Mao Xing, Hexing, Yuda, Dafeng, Shenji, and Renfeng buying to cover short positions. New Cotton Enters the Market, Yarn and Cotton Instead Feel Firm and Expensive: A Look at the Situation Over the Past Two Weeks 185

The yarn and cotton situation over the past two weeks has been characterized by intense competition between the bulls and bears. Many of the former bulls, recognizing that domestic cotton production is abundant, estimated at 16 million dan, more than double last year, have liquidated their long positions and turned bearish. Tongji, Dafu, and Yuda, who previously absorbed the most volume, have now become short sellers, with the largest short positions. The industry believes that this year's harvest will be plentiful, farmers' finances will improve, and yarn sales will be optimistic. With the pacification of the situation in Guangdong and Guangxi, customer purchases have been very active recently, and factories have mostly sold out of spot yarn. Yarn inventories in yarn and cloth warehouses have gradually decreased from 37,000 bales to 26,000 bales. With the flourishing trade in fabrics, the yarn market is becoming increasingly solid. The yarn and cotton market is therefore hovering. In fact, with the entry of new cotton into the market, raw materials are expected to be cheaper, cotton yarn costs are lower, and profits are possible. Furthermore, many of the yarn factories that had suspended operations have resumed work with the availability of new cotton, gradually increasing production. In addition, foreign merchants are fiercely competing for sales in the market, and with the passing of the autumn sales season, it may be difficult to sell at good prices, so there are quite a few people selling forward contracts. Cotton factories report that their inventories of Chen cotton are thin, so they are eagerly competing for new cotton, with a strong need. However, they have no intention of trying long-term cotton. However, market prices in various production areas are higher than in Shanghai, so shipments to Shanghai are still scarce. Currently, the weather is favorable, and off-market selling is strong. Yarn sales are still good, and prices are rising daily, so factories continue to purchase raw cotton. The recent yarn and cotton market prices for the past two weeks are listed below.
