Chunqiu

Tidbits 211

— (Ba Ling)

It is said that in Shanghai, due to various reasons, several people commit suicide by drowning in the Huangpu River or by other means every day. If this is true, then the issue of suicide is indeed a serious social problem that we absolutely cannot ignore.

Speaking of the reasons for suicide, if analyzed, they are roughly nothing more than the two major elements of "love" and "life." Indeed, food and sex are the two major needs of life. Some people commit suicide because they cannot solve their livelihood problems, while others commit suicide because of changes in their love lives. On the surface, these two reasons seem to make the former more serious. However, in my opinion, no matter what, suicide is never the right way. A history of life, thoroughly speaking, is a history of struggle. We must struggle every day we live. Those who have solved the problems of food and sex should, of course, struggle. But those who have not solved their livelihood problems should especially strive. Only those who struggle have a place to live in society. You must know that bread will not fall from the sky. Once you understand this, then you will see how unreasonable suicide is.

Mr. Tao Xingzhi said: "Life comes for a great cause and should leave after completing a great cause." This is very true. Everyone has a mission in life. Since we are humans with round heads and square toes, then we must do something beneficial to ourselves and society. It is really wrong to take suicide as a "one and done" action after encountering some setbacks.

Friends: We should firmly remember the famous saying: "Life is for great causes, and we should leave after accomplishing some achievements."

Talking About Horses 212

— Shijiu

Speaking of horses, they have always been valued by people throughout history. "Trading a beloved concubine for a horse" is sung in the Music Bureau poems and is a popular story. This is one. Also, throughout history, which famous general has not had a beloved horse to depend on for life, sharing happiness and hardship together? This is two. Therefore, the selection of horse breeds has always been a matter of concern for people, which is of course. According to our country, horse breeds have always been inferior to others. In the past, countries such as Dayuan produced famous horses, as seen in various notes. Recently, the world's best horse breeds are undoubtedly those from Arabia, with those from Mongolia still trailing behind. The advantages of Arabian horses are their strong feet and tall height. Strong feet mean they can race with cars; tall height means they can leap over a person's head. Moreover, they are intelligent and sensitive. Once trained, they obey their masters' orders. They are so rare and valuable that the Arabs treat their horses as their second lives, with the idea of "not valuing children but valuing horses." Each horse is worth between five or six thousand gold to ten thousand gold. Male horses are especially valuable because they can crossbreed and spread the breed.

The price for a foreign horse to mate with an Arabian male horse is also considerable. It is said that the Arabian horse owner can get as much as five or six hundred gold for each time. However, a famous breed cannot be obtained from just one mating. It must go through six or seven times before it can be no different from a pure Arabian horse. For example, if there is a mare from the Hao Ancient breed, after mating with an Arabian male horse, the offspring happens to be a filly. When it grows up, another Arabian male horse is selected to mate with it, and the offspring is again a filly. Only after going through this six or seven times can that horse—whether male or female—have the same qualities and physique as a true Arabian horse.

It is said that our country's certain institutions only have a dozen or so pure Arabian horses, which are used exclusively for mating. The feeding cost of each horse per day is more than two gold, which is enough for the daily expenses of an eight-member family. It really makes people's tongues wag and sigh, "Humans are not as good as horses!"

Big Guy 213

— Yingzi

The residents around Penglai Road, when mentioning the chubby, buoyant-looking Big Guy, almost everyone knows him. Especially the students of Meixi, Xicheng, Aiqun, and Shangwen elementary schools nearby are even more familiar with him. Therefore, in this vicinity, the name of Big Guy can truly be said to be famous far and wide, known to all women.

Regardless of whether it is sunny, raining, windy, or snowing, Big Guy always sets up his stall all year round, diligently doing his very low-income job, without a hint of weariness or a trace of complaint, always smiling.

His stall is fully stocked with candies, toys, and bread snacks. In winter, there are baked squid and boiled rice cakes. In summer, there are even more ice cream and sour plum soup. Therefore, although it is a small stall, it can be said to have everything.

Elementary school students are his only major customers. Dismissal time is also the main time for his business. During this time, he is very busy dealing with these small customers.

Big Guy, although engaged in this petty occupation, has been working hard all year round. Now he has accumulated some money and has entered another stage, opening a shop and becoming a boss. The reason he has reached this point today is entirely due to his perseverance and hard-working spirit!

Hometown Red Swastika Society 214

— Sisu

Fortunately, in our hometown—Taixian County—a branch of the World Red Swastika Society has been organized. Helpless poor people will not be displaced, and there is a relief organization in the event of natural disasters.

Managing local charitable undertakings depends entirely on getting the right people. So-called getting the right people, business ability is secondary. First, the person in charge must have a truly compassionate and self-sacrificing spirit, with only the locality in their eyes, not themselves, in order to not betray the original intention of charity. The president of the Taixian Red Swastika Society branch is Mr. De Liang, the esteemed father of Cao Mengyu. He is also the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, and has been re-elected for ten years, unable to refuse. The reason is that, in addition to presiding over the Red Swastika Society to carry out charitable undertakings, he is also relied upon to uphold justice and resolve disputes, and all the merchants and people do not allow him to get away with it. Mr. De Liang has repeatedly wanted to get rid of the Chamber of Commerce and devote himself to charitable undertakings, but it is impossible.

The Taixian Red Swastika Society branch, due to the small size of the meeting place, has decided to build a large building with more than 20 rooms, which requires about 15,000 yuan. More than 10,000 yuan have already been donated by various parties, but because disaster relief has been advanced and released, it is not enough. Until now, members have found an opportunity to complete it. It turns out that this autumn is Mr. De Liang's sixtieth birthday, and it has been publicly agreed to celebrate his birthday and use the banquet funds to pay for construction costs. However, whether Mr. De Liang agrees is still unknown. Although we are traveling abroad now, for the sake of our hometown society, we very much hope that it can be realized!

Swapping a Phoenix's Nest 215

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Six: Iron Face Sees Close Relatives, Words Hide from Parrots; Moth Eyebrows Hold Chivalry, Pawnshop Asks About Kunlun

Youmei laughed again, shook her head twice, and said: Because you are still very traditional, I can't just say anything. Menglan had a very righteous face and nodded to him twice, saying: What you said to me is all from the heart, and I am very grateful. However, I have my own private opinion. First, no matter what I do, I want to take care of my personality. Second, although I myself cannot make meaningless sacrifices, I also do not want to sacrifice others to fulfill my private plans. Hearing him say this, Youmei supported the table with her left hand, supported her cheek, and touched a pencil on the table with her right hand, knocking it on the table with the back of the pencil. She stared at a copy of Jiangnan Magazine spread out on the table, lost in thought. Menglan, because her eyes were focused, did not understand what it meant, so he said: This is the latest publication, do you have it? Youmei said: I am not like you who is obsessed with magazines. I buy one to read when I have time. If I miss the issue and don't buy it, then so be it. But why are you so enthusiastic? Menglan said: It's not that I'm particularly enthusiastic about magazines, it's just that I'm sitting at home all day, very bored, and I only borrow these few magazines to relieve the boredom in my chest. Youmei said: Do you like to read the novels in this magazine? Or do you like old essays? Menglan said: Of course, I like to read novels. Youmei said: Which writer in the magazine do you admire the most now? Menglan said: I read magazines just to browse, and after reading them, I throw them aside. I don't care who is good and who is bad. Youmei laughed: Relatively speaking, who has a deeper impression on you? Menglan said, why do you keep asking about this, I find it a bit strange. After he finished saying this, his face was not so natural, which was a mistake on his part, but Youmei was a little suspicious. (Seven Eight)

Formidable Enemy of the Pawnshop Industry 216

— Xiaoxia

I met a friend, Mr. Mou, who is in the pawnshop industry. He lamented that the pawnshop industry has been declining in recent years, and that the golden age of the pawnshop industry has passed. Because more items are pawned than redeemed, and the outlet for pawned goods is also sluggish. I asked about the situation of redeeming pawns for customers in the past two years and the impact on the pawnshop industry. According to him, the method of redeeming pawns for customers was first planned and implemented by Lu Shui, the owner of Lu Tianbao in Dapuqiao. Although it was only advertised in small advertisements in newspapers, there were many people in the society who held pawn tickets. Therefore, in recent years, gold, diamonds, jewelry, and jade that have not been redeemed when the term expired have been as rare as phoenix feathers. Pawnshops hope that the owner will redeem the items pawned in order to earn interest. However, gold, diamonds, jewelry, and jade are expected to be pawned out when the term expires because of the low cost and high profit. Now, this benefit has been taken away by the gold store and returned to the owner of the item, which is like a formidable enemy of the pawnshop industry.

Two Famous Products of Guangdong 217

— Wu Jiren

Yesterday, I was invited by Mr. Zhao Zemin to drink at his new residence. The dishes were very rich. One dish was olive-braised dace, which tasted very delicious. I had never tasted this dish in my life, so I asked the host. According to him: Olives are very cheap to make in Guangdong because they are produced there, and this thing is widely used. The olive kernels required for Crown Garden mooncakes are purchased in bulk from there. Because olive production is quite rich and the demand is quite large, the dish used today is locally called "oil-extracted olive corner". My friends from Guangdong brought it here. Hongkou in Shanghai also sells it. When it is first made, the green olives are cut in half at the waist, and the kernels in the pits are used to make mooncakes. It is said that each load is about 80 taels of gold this year. In previous years, when the harvest was small, it was as expensive as 130 to 140. The so-called "oil-extracted olive corner" is made by first paying salt-preserved and dried the olive meat, reading the date, and drying it extremely. Then, it is soaked in "oil-extracted oil" (that is, the top-quality soy sauce here, also known as white oil). Soak it for two days, and then dry it again. Do this twice and it is done. Not only will it not change for a long time, but it is also very delicious to use it to cook dishes. When used with porridge, you only need to add soy sauce, sugar, and a little raw oil to mix it. The fragrance is refreshing, and olives are cool in nature, so eating them for a long time is good for the body. I am happy to record it.

Also, He Chumei, the head of the wholesale department of Crown Garden, has lived in the south for generations. His ancestors were doctors, especially proficient in ophthalmology, so there is the "Bird Gold Eye Medicine" that has been sold at home and abroad for 150 years. The other day, my wife had an eye disease, and she was given several bottles of this product. After applying it for a week, the redness in her eyes completely subsided. Mr. He said: "It is still popular far from Nanyang, Europe, and the United States, and close to China and South China. Old and young people in Guangdong especially know that He Tongren's 'Bird Gold Eye Medicine' is a famous and valuable medicine." Now the four major companies in Shanghai also sell it on consignment, and it is also selling well in Beijing, Hangzhou, Suzhou, and Wuxi. According to Mr. He: Eye diseases are the most difficult to treat, because the eyes belong to the kidneys. If the kidney water is insufficient, the eyes will be confused. This bird gold can still be cured when it is about to go blind, and it is especially effective for red eyes and insufficient eyesight after a sleepless night, as well as for the weakening eyesight of the elderly. It can be completely cured and can also be applied to external symptoms to achieve results.

World News

Japan's Scheduled World Games 218

— Jiyun

Ever since the next World Games were decided to be held in Tokyo, Japan, the Japanese have been very excited. Because it coincides with the 2,600th anniversary of Japan's founding, the opportunity is very rare. On the one hand, the Japanese know that after the World Games are held in Tokyo, the income will be considerable, so they believe that the World Games are the only opportunity to make a fortune. They calculated that the Lausanne Games had an income of 150 million yen, and this time Berlin can get 100 million yen. Although Tokyo is farther from Europe and the United States, the enthusiasm of foreigners for sightseeing in Japan and the low price of Japanese silver dollars are enough to attract visitors. In this Berlin Games, there were about 300,000 foreign spectators. In Japan, because of the Commemorative Exposition, there will be at least 100,000 people, which will cost about 100 million yen in Tokyo. In addition, there were only 3,000 athletes in Lausanne. This time, 53 countries participated, reaching 6,000 people. In Tokyo, with 3,000 people calculated, the average cost per person is 2,000 yen, then 6 million yen is needed. The Japanese are also flocking to see the Games, so there will be no less than one million visitors from various places. The average cost per person is 50 yen, totaling 50 million yen. Therefore, according to their budget, the World Games can send a huge amount of 256 million yen into the hands of Tokyo people.

Newspapers and magazines also often introduce the opportunities to make a fortune during the World Games. The Japanese are experts in small-scale business. At that time, restaurants, cigarette shops, hotels, amusement parks, toy stores, etc. will definitely make their speculative business a big deal.

Due to years of expanding its military, Japan's construction projects in recent years have not been as good as in the years after the Great Earthquake. The provinces, seeing the military's expenses expand without limit, all want to take the opportunity to expand once. Four years later, the 2,600th anniversary of the founding of the country and the World Games will bring double happiness. Various construction projects can be renovated, and the military will have to dare to be angry but dare not speak out. The current budget is 10.4 million yen for the venue, 6.8 million yen for the renovation of Tokyo Station, 10 million yen for road construction, 1 million yen for the Olympic Village, 10 million yen for the City Hall, and other projects such as the National Museum, the Exposition venue, and the Founding Memorial Hall. Various projects cost at least about 60 million yen.

Anything can become a business in Japan. Holding the World Games in Japan is a big business for all Tokyo people, so it is called the "God of Fortune." It is estimated that for the World Games, Tokyo's construction and expenses will reach 300 million yen. The 6 million citizens of Tokyo will get an average of 50 yen per person. The profit-seeking Japanese, hearing that such a huge amount of money will come to Tokyo, are of course overjoyed.

Local Customs

Chicken Feather Shops in Beiping 219

— Sheli

In the northern country, the cold is as sharp as a knife.

Well-off people put on heavy fur coats. The whole family, big and small, surround the stove and drink two cups, creating a "Nine Nine Cold Dissipation Picture". How comfortable! What if you're bored in the house? Take a chartered car to the cinema. There are radiators there.

As for the poor men and women who have become beggars, they don't have the blessing to surround the stove to dissipate the cold. The cinema won't allow them in. During the day, they huddle up in the cold wind, begging lords, ladies, young masters, and young misses for a penny. At night, they rush to the chicken feather shop.

Chicken feather shops are a specialty of Beiping and a blessing for beggars!

They are mostly located outside Tianqiao Hademen. You can't find their traces in the bustling urban areas. The rent is too expensive there! Beggars come here to sleep for a night. In the past, it was only three big [coins] (a big coin is two small copper coins), but now? It's up! One big coin! (That is, one copper coin worth paying Ganwen), if it doesn't rise, it will lose its capital.

Here, there are no eyes like Naoma Xila, no steam from radiators, and no rich wine fragrance. It's just a simple house filled with chicken feathers and chicken shit stench. There are no berths. People come and lie on the ground at will, covering their heads and bodies with chicken feathers. The unbearable cold!

Singers, fortune tellers, lotus drummers, people with broken legs, people with missing hands, blind people without eyes, patients with dropsy... They have all become brothers sleeping together.

When it gets cold, the chicken feather shop opens its doors, and every night, the customers are always squeezed in.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talking Points

Center of European Political Activity Moves to Geneva 220

— I

Geneva, 20th - The center of European political activity will move to Geneva tomorrow, as the League of Nations General Assembly will open in a highly threatening environment to hold important meetings. I think this kind of meeting will not have much effect, because the driving force behind Europe's precarious state lies entirely in Germany and Italy. Germany has withdrawn from the League of Nations, and Italy has also withdrawn in an invisible way. This kind of political activity is only a one-sided activity of those who advocate democracy.

So, in terms of the overall picture of Europe? Europe is now divided into two major factions, one is the democratic faction, and the other is the fascist faction. If neither of these two opposing flags can be withdrawn or overthrown, then there will be no peace in Europe. To put it bluntly, the first faction advocates preserving colonies, and the second faction advocates redistributing colonies. In short, it is just a colonial problem. Under the current circumstances, neither side is willing to give in easily. The result can only be resolved with airplanes and artillery fire. The paper tiger of Geneva has long been exposed. Even if it is repaired, it must be repaired in a way that one bag is replaced with another, and one bag is worse than the other.

I take a step back and talk about the inside story of the League of Nations. What the League of Nations should urgently solve now is the Spanish Civil War, the war between Nuremberg and Moscow, the global frenzy of rearmament, and the tense situation in Palestine. All of these will be ominous backgrounds in the discussion of this decision by the General Assembly. However, if none of these serious issues are raised for direct discussion, then the reopening of this decision by the League of Nations General Assembly can be said to be a waste of money, time, and effort. The result will definitely be the same as when our country's athletes attended the World Games, eating a few dumplings and dispersing. I think this is a futile effort.

Secondly, the issue of the representative of Abyssinia attending The Credentials Committee appointed by the General Assembly to review the credentials of representatives of various countries. Among them, the credentials of the representative of Abyssinia are the most difficult. Geneva reported again on the 21st that Abyssinia requested to attend the League of Nations General Assembly. Several major member states of the League of Nations have preconceived notions. The Credentials Committee should refuse Abyssinia's request under the pretext, so that all representatives are unwilling to serve as members of the Credentials Committee. From this issue alone, it can be seen that the League of Nations itself has lost its qualification to exist. When Italy invaded Abyssinia, the League of Nations resolved that Italy was an aggressor country. When Italy captured the Abyssinian capital and the Italian king concurrently held the title of Emperor of Abyssinia, the League of Nations did not recognize it. Then Abyssinia's qualification as a member state of the League of Nations clearly still exists and has not been revoked. Then how can the League of Nations refuse to accept Abyssinia as a member state of the League of Nations when it decides to hold a meeting? Now that the League of Nations is meeting, and the representative of Abyssinia is being refused attendance, I really don't know what the reason is?

However, the mouthpiece of Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, the famous reporter Gaige, recently published an article in the Italian Daily, which roughly said that as long as the Abyssinian delegation is in Geneva, Italy will not participate in the work of the League of Nations. Although Italy does not seek recognition of its sovereignty over Abyssinia, Italy cannot recognize a group of exiles who come out to represent this regime. From these two things alone, does the League of Nations still have value in holding meetings? Can the League of Nations still achieve practical results in holding meetings? Therefore, I think it's better not to hold them.

A Visit to the Mudu Chastity Preservation Bureau (Part 2) 221

— Fang Zhou

(Special Feature from This Newspaper) Their ages are all advanced, the oldest being around sixty or seventy, and the youngest over forty. I walked out from the door on the right side of the Buddhist hall and saw a virtuous widow in her twenties cooking. Beside her were two elderly women, one folding tin foil, and the other doing laundry. So I greeted the woman doing laundry, hoping to inquire about the bureau's clerk. She turned out to be a woman from a respectable family and very talkative. She generously pulled up a bamboo chair for me to sit on, and then introduced me to the young woman cooking and the old woman folding tin foil. It turned out they were mother and daughter-in-law. Because the daughter-in-law's husband had died and she wished to remain chaste here, her mother-in-law had also come to live with her.

First, she told me that Mr. Lin from here had gone to Guangfu on business. Then, she told me about the general situation of the bureau, as she had been here for over thirty years and knew a lot. She spoke of the bureau's decline and current financial difficulties, expressing a sense of deep emotion for the past.

While telling me, she also invited me to see their rooms, saying that the rooms here were originally very large, but many places were collapsing.

As we were looking at those empty, collapsing houses, Mr. Lin returned from Guangfu. So, after he invited me to the reception room, he told me about the bureau's past and present situation. The bureau originally had no fixed basic funding, only donations from various parties. There used to be some, but now they have completely stopped. Even the ten donation tickets from this county can only collect three hundred cash per ticket each month. All the bureau's regular expenses, in addition to the rent rice collected from the five hundred mu of bureau-owned land, and some coffin storage fees from the Lingyan Funeral Home at the foot of Mount Shengyan, there is nothing else produced.

In recent years, land rent has been very difficult to collect. Even rents from three or four years ago have not yet been collected, so the bureau's finances have become difficult. Because of this, the bureau had to tighten its expenses, reducing one of the original four clerks. The Lingyan Elementary School attached to the bureau has also been closed, and the widows' children have all gone to the county elementary school to study. All the costs of books and other expenses are borne by the widows themselves, and the widows' daily vegetables have also been reduced to a pitiful amount!

There are currently more than thirty widows in the bureau, with a total of more than forty people, all from this county. It is said that in the past, when there were the most, there were seventy or eighty people here. Widows who wish to enter the bureau must have a guarantor recommend them and fill out an investigation form. After the bureau investigates and confirms that their family background is truly clean and that they are helpless widows, they can enter the bureau. Those with young children or elderly aunts are also allowed to bring them, but they must pay an entrance fee of more than two yuan when entering the bureau for the purpose of tidying the house. After entering the bureau, the bureau provides a room. Apart from food, the bureau does not bear any other expenses. In the past, the bureau was responsible for the widows' old age, death, and illness, but now it has been completely abolished. The money the widows earn from their own work is theirs to keep. After death, their relatives must come to collect the body for burial, or a collection will be taken up locally. Those whose own children have grown up and wish to start a family and leave the bureau are allowed to do so, but they must also pay an exit fee of more than two yuan to pay for tidying up the house.

Normally, widows cannot go out casually except to go shopping. If they need to visit relatives or travel far and must stay overnight, they must apply to the clerk and obtain permission before being allowed, but there are restrictions, only once a month, and they cannot exceed the prescribed date. Any widow who violates the rules will be ordered to leave the bureau.

It is said that the rules of the Chastity Preservation Bureau were originally very strict, but now they are not as strict as they used to be, and recently there have been almost no lonely widows requesting to enter the bureau.

Closing Down 222

— Ding Ni

Morning.

The accountant strode in and slammed the fake mahogany dresser so hard it echoed: "Rent! Rent! You said you'd pay today, how many months are you paying?"

Mr. Li, who was wiping the uneven mirror on the wardrobe with a tattered cloth, jumped up as if an orange had burned his butt, pleadingly: "Accountant, to tell you the truth, this woodworking trade of ours is much harder than before. Young people nowadays, they all want mo... modern things, they don't like my fake mahogany..."

"Stop rambling, how about the rent?" The accountant's air was like a father scolding his son.

"Sir, there's really no way, no way, please forgive me..."

"What nonsense, four months' rent... forgive... bullshit!"

"...no way... for... forgive." Mr. Li was sweating profusely, holding a rag, unable to think of any pleading words. A bead of sweat fell into his eye, causing a sharp pain, so he picked up the rag to wipe his eyes, leaving several black lines on his eyelid.

The two gatekeepers standing behind the accountant, holding rent tickets, almost burst out laughing at the scene. But the accountant didn't even have a hint of a smile, his face ashen: "Bullshit! Bullshit! I give you until lunchtime to send three months' rent to the accounting office, or I'll come and seal the door tomorrow!" - Saying that, he put the pencil on his ear and left.

Three months' rent, three times three is nine, three times six is eighteen, one hundred and eight yuan. Upstairs in the chest, there are forty-three yuan that A-Ju kept for her dowry, and... and the eight yuan of wages for A-Xiang the cook in my waistband for last month, a total of fifty-one yuan. How is that enough? Thinking of this, Mr. Li's heart felt like hemp.

Although he thought of the wooden furniture in the shop... But...

Next door, Yu Chang Pawnshop "stopped accepting wooden furniture."

Mr. Li didn't eat lunch, sitting on the stool in a daze like a lost soul. His mind was thinking of many things... someone losing a wallet at the door... an aviation lottery ticket...

"Why didn't you take it when I told you to take it at lunchtime?"

Thinking it was the accountant, Mr. Li jumped up again as if the stool had burned his butt. He looked closely, it wasn't the accountant, it was the gatekeeper A-Wang.

"Brother A-Wang, you know the suffering of poor people, please say a word for me to the accountant, and ask him to give me a few days' grace."

"How can that be? To be honest, even the accountant can't make the decision, the foreigners above are urging us very hard. You still have to think of a way..."

"What way is there to think of? I've borrowed from everyone I can borrow from."

A-Wang's attitude was as amiable as Jie Tou asking Mr. Li for wine money: "We're all barefoot people... it's not like there's no way..." Whispering in his ear, mumbling a few words: "Your wooden furniture is worth more than this, and if you sue, sealing the door and stuff, it won't look good on their faces..."

Mr. Li took thirty-three yuan from the forty-three yuan dowry money in the chest and gave it to A-Wang. A-Wang, A-Ju, and her mother stood aside, shedding tears. Mr. Li wanted to ask A-Wang for the rent ticket. A-Wang said: "The rent ticket has been taken to the new government office, if you want it, you have to take a trip there."

After A-Wang left, Mr. Li instructed the staff to tidy up their things.

The next morning, Mr. Li had already settled all his things—the fake mahogany furniture—in his maternal uncle's courtyard. He sighed there from time to time.

He didn't eat lunch. He told A-Ju's mother that he was going outside to look for a shop location and went out.

He searched for most of the day, but couldn't agree on a single place. Rent was too expensive in busy areas, and cheaper places weren't good.

On the way home, he passed by the front of his shop. Many people were there, pointing and gesturing, saying: "...the market is depressed... this furniture shop, it was doing well yesterday, but now it's moved away, there's nothing left..."

The words Mr. Li heard filled him with sadness, almost bringing him to tears. He saw that the shop door was open, and the accountant was talking to someone. He squeezed in to hear what the accountant was saying?

"...the lowest price, four months' rent, two floors put on top of three floors, very well built, at least seven or eight yuan if you make new ones, now we're asking you for thirty yuan, ten yuan is the opening fee, if you want to take over, at least..."

The person standing opposite the accountant shook his head: "I only plan to offer one hundred yuan..."

Mr. Li ran away filled with grievances. He understood A-Wang's kindness in advising him to move out that night.

Child Brides in Southern Fujian 223

— Li Tian

Like elsewhere, women are looked down upon in our Southern Fujian. "Obedient at home, obedient to her husband after marriage, and obedient to her son in old age," "If you marry a chicken, you follow the chicken, if you marry a dog, you follow the dog." These shackles—so-called virtues—imposed on women by feudal society still hold firm in the minds of the general public. Especially the notion that daughters can't produce wealth and will eventually marry out, even wealthy families in the city, except for the first pregnancy, mostly "marry out" their daughters within three days of birth. At that time, the parents only need to spend a little money to prepare some clothes for her, and buy some rouge, lead powder, taro, bananas, pears, oranges, lotus candles, cotton, "beautiful face" flowers, sugar balls, raw pork, pork bones, and bean cakes as customary dowry items, put them in a red basket, and together with the daughter, give the midwife a baby to any family—the in-laws—and consider their responsibility as parents complete. They treat their own daughters like doing business, thinking that even if they are raised, getting a few hundred dollars of betrothal money is not worth it.

Besides small citizens in the city, almost every corner of the countryside has people adopting child brides, one or two or three at a time. Even landlords and wealthy farmers do this; especially those without sons need them even more. Because they can hope that the child bride will bring in a capable man in the future to carry on the family line. People who sever their descendants are usually despised: even if they have not committed any evil deeds in this life, people will add that their "previous life" must have been a deeply sinful person. Moreover, adopting a child bride does not require much care: it only takes a little time each day to breastfeed or feed. In addition, they leave the ignorant little baby in the cradle to cry, to soak in shit and urine. They don't feel any guilt for treating the little daughter-in-law like this, because they themselves were raised like this. They also know that their own daughters are treated the same in other people's homes, but they don't care. The so-called "at home, praying for sandalwood, out of home, firewood in the fire alley," means that daughters can be as precious as sandalwood at home, but once married out, they are like firewood in the fire alley that no one wants to burn, arbitrarily abandoned. If unfortunately the child bride dies halfway, the adopter will of course attribute it to fate, and even the parents will only sigh: saying that their own daughter has a bad life, no luck. Because child brides can be arbitrarily abused, their death rate is shockingly high! According to general estimates, among those who are raised to adulthood and can marry or bring in a man, at most only three or four out of ten.

But raising a child bride is not just to reduce the burden when she is an adult. When the child bride reaches the age of five or six, the in-laws can not give her a penny and whip her to clean the house, pick up fallen leaves, and take care of the little husband, little brothers-in-law, or little sisters-in-law, etc. After another year or two, everything comes. Washing diapers, cooking, carrying firewood and rice, holding children, feeding livestock... everything is done: but she has no luck with food and clothing. But child brides are treated in many different ways! Even in her mother's house, if she was born in the year of the "Tiger," or if the fortune-telling blind man determined that her "fate" was clashing with something or bad, she will of course not be tolerated by her mother's family and will be thrown out earlier. Once she arrives at her husband's house, she will not only be particularly despised, but if a death occurs, she will be even worse off; she will not only be considered the one who "clashed" with them and be abused, but will often freeze to death or starve to death because she is not taken care of. But what does this poor little baby understand?

Speaking of their marriage, it is also very miserable. Their marriage often starts at the age of fourteen or fifteen; sometimes at these ages, they already have a child in their arms. Most of them have not gone through any marriage ceremony, and some only hold a perfunctory ceremony after giving birth. Those who are in-laws are all filled with eager thoughts of holding a grandson. Because once there is a grandson, when they die, they can write "Great-Grandfather of Three Generations" or "Great-Grandmother of Three Generations" on the white lantern. If they adopt another granddaughter-in-law to raise, they can even write "Great-Grandfather and Great-Grandmother of Four Generations." Even if they are too poor to buy a coffin, people will still call him or her "lucky," and they also seem to be able to die in peace. Therefore, they are not worried about the behavior of their daughter-in-law before marriage. Child brides, with very few exceptions, also think that they have already become someone's daughter-in-law, and have been designated as the wife of a certain son of their in-laws, so they have no choice but to let that unmarried man dispose of her. Even before development is complete, it is difficult to escape, because those who are future husbands are mostly five or six years or more than ten years older than themselves. If the in-laws don't have a son themselves, they are also filled with hope of bringing in a capable man as soon as possible! First, to reduce suffering, second, to have a grandson to hold, and third, to avoid making the little daughter-in-law cause trouble. In this way, little daughters-in-law often have to live a sexual life with a stranger when they are just developing. They have no freedom to choose at all, and the sadness they feel can only be endured in their hearts. If the man is not happy, then she will have to be sold around like a "tomb tree." Their lives are dark.

Ballad Singing 226

Cao Xiaoying's Jade Dragonfly

China-West (1040) 1:00 PM to 1:45 PM

Opening Chapter "Guan Suifeng's Night Visit to the Tiger's Den"

The affairs of the world are like a game of chess. The vicissitudes of fortune sigh at floating dust. Since ancient times, how many infatuated lovers. Having read the vicissitudes of life, I feel the ancient and the present. I think I am, a chivalrous heart and proud bones. Wandering the rivers and lakes for ten springtimes. I sigh at my humble life as a mayfly. I am used to speaking out injustices in the world. Jia Shu is, a romantic young master in love with Fengxi. Utter affection, utter love. Before leaving, he entrusted her with a heavy emotional burden. Tell her to always keep a bit of his heart. Who knew that Fengxi was, a flower bud envied by the wind and rain. Who will come to be a guardian bell for the flower? He only regrets, mistakenly entering the tiger's den, her beauty trapped. Spring locked heavy doors, no one seen. Letting her tears drip like cuckoos crying at the night moon. Embroidered curtains silent, weeping at dusk. Fortunately, his secret mother transmitted news. Suddenly touching the heroic ear with a start. Therefore, he risked his life to explore the tiger's den. There are walls with ears, secrets heard from over the wall. Secretly watching that, the general does not change his crazy slave-like state. Sometimes, he begs others with a humble and flattering look. And the pearl-stringed curios are dazzling. Ya Qin is entrusted to mediate. Unexpectedly, the daughter loves golden objects. She only values gold, not affection. Since ancient times, the battlefield of love has many strange states. Gold is good for buying beautiful women's hearts. If I had known, mirror flowers and water moons are empty shadows. I would not have, doubted and suspected, falsely acting as true. But I, seeing the situation, am always filled with grief. It is difficult to suppress the raging tide for a time. I can't wait to cut off this love seed for you. Don't betray the long-term trust. Alas, the young master Zhong quietly like in a dream. Tragically turning the consequences into previous causes. Therefore, a letter is sent by post. Suddenly making him say goodbye to his parents and hasten his journey. It does not prevent, sending a message to those who have lost their love in the battlefield of love.

Xing Ruiting's Three Smiles

Lin Ji (1220) 9:05 PM to 10:00 PM

Opening Chapter "The Explanation of Romanticism"

One point of talent, one point of affection. Who is heartless, who is affectionate. Beauties cannot help but love talented men. Talented men also love beauties. But there is one thing that is hateful. Affection is long or short, not uniform. There are also, those who are difficult to see when they are usually affectionate. There are also. Those who are unintentionally intimate. There are also, those who start by messing around and end by abandoning. There are also, those who first become Wu and Yue and then become married. It's not that people's hearts are thick or thin. It's just because talent is shallow or deep. How can this change start today? There were many who came before. Admirable is, Song Hong not abandoning his old wife. Lovely is, Lechang holding a mirror not remarrying, Detestable is, Li Yi heartlessly forgetting old favors. Disgusting is, Wang Kui intentionally betraying his previous oath. Wheat can be intimate with willows. Poems inscribed on leaves also become marriages. It's ridiculous that the world is confused and doesn't wake up. Secretly stealing jade and fragrance is considered normal. Dewy couples recognize it as true. What's the use of fighting for love and jealousy. Suddenly causing turmoil is not peaceful. It's ridiculous, not understanding the two words of romanticism. Boasting of being talented men and beauties. Isn't it the opposite of being misled by romanticism? Yangtai is not a romantic pavilion. Making romanticism a matter of truth. However, affection is not romanticism. Even if romanticism is a few points lighter. I advise all talented men of romanticism. There is no talent, no affection. Forcing romanticism to explain affection. It is a sin of romanticism. Where you can find pleasure, find pleasure.

Good scenery. Some are getting drunk and playing with the moon. Some are carrying the moon in a small boat. Some are strolling in the suburbs to watch the bright moon. Some are playing with the moon and reciting the wind into a drunken land. There is also that once-a-year Mid-Autumn Moon. Meeting that beautiful scenery and good time, busy playing with the moon. Seeing that the moon is white and the flowers are fragrant, it is really happy. It is even more happy to play with beauties. The most wonderful thing is to visit the Moon Palace within the Guanghan Palace. Talking with Chang'e in the moon. A song of neon clothes sings in the moon. Feather clothes dance out of the Moon Palace room. A humble cold moon steals new tunes. Unfortunately, it is difficult to climb the Mingyue Hall. Therefore, every time I enjoy the moon, I think of neon clothes.

Movie News

"Women's Rights" Premieres Tonight 228

The Star Film Company's great production of the year "Women's Rights" premieres tonight at 9:15 PM at the Jincheng Grand Theater. "Women's Rights" is directed by Zhang Shichuan, starring Ms. Hu Die, who has been away from the screen for a long time. Zhao Dan, Yan Yuexian, Gong Jianong, Ye Qiuxin, Mei Xi, Shu Xiwen, Wang Xianzhai, Yuan Shaomei, Wang Zhengxin, and Lu Luming co-star. Hong Shen wrote the screenplay, depicting a woman who has received a university education who is unaccustomed to the powdered air of a young mistress and leaps into society, from a bank clerk, a female teacher, to a female worker, suffering all kinds of setbacks. Although she returns to her pink dreams, she finally feels the emptiness of women's status and walks away in the night wind. The description is moving, and the performance is tonight. After the screening, it will continue to be screened tomorrow. The new autumn is a good time for watching movies, and "Women's Rights" is currently the best film, and people from all walks of life should be happy to watch it.

Li Lili's scene will be screened tomorrow night at the same time in Caden Xinguang

Dance Film "Flying Swallow Leans on New Makeup" 229

Opens tomorrow at the Shanghai Grand Theater

Art and Culture Notes 230

"Little Sisters" is scheduled to premiere at the Xinguang Grand Theater in this city on Double Ten Day. Seven or eight theaters in other provinces have also scheduled it for simultaneous screening. The Art and Culture copy room is working day and night to make seven or eight copies, which will be sent to various ports in the near future.

"Incarnation" "Girl" has been renamed "Incarnation Girl Sequel" after a script meeting. It is still written by Huang Jiamo and directed by Fang Bolin. In addition to the original cast of "Incarnation Girl" working together, the famous villain Wang Naidong has also been added. He plays a gentleman with a mask.

Exterior scenes for "Good Luck Comes to the Door" are currently being filmed in Wuxi. The crew and actors, numbering fifty or sixty, and more than a hundred pieces of costumes and props, set off yesterday. Everything is scheduled, and the work is very tense.

Wu Weiyun, a former colleague of Art and Culture, is now a major photographer in the Nanchang Headquarters. He came to Shanghai a few days ago to buy goods, fully armed and full of luck. Yuan Meiyun, Chen Kengran, Wang Yin, and Xu Qinfang have been inviting him to banquets in recent days, which is very lively.
